3. Didi is not popular in Kashgar. If you need to take a taxi, call the front desk. They provide us with a taxi service.
4. Opposite is the Xiledao Amusement Park, which is very suitable for families with children like us to come and stay. When we are tired after playing, we can cross the road and go back to the hotel to rest.
